AARCH64 GAS  C:\Users\ldebo\AppData\Local\Temp\ccAQ5mmN.s 			page 2


  46:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	if (mode < 0 || mode > ALTFUNC3) return false;					// Check requested mode is valid, return false 
  47:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	uint32_t bit = 1 << ((gpio % 10) * 3);							// Create bit mask

 120:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	} else {														// Falling edge detect

 152:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** /*-[timer_getTickCount]-----------------------------------------------------}
 153:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  Get 1Mhz ARM system timer tick count in full 64 bit.
 154:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  The timer read is as per the Broadcom specification of two 32bit reads
 155:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  RETURN: tickcount value as an unsigned 64bit value
 156:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  30Jun17 LdB
 157:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  --------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
 158:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** uint64_t timer_getTickCount (void) {
 159:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	uint64_t resVal;
AARCH64 GAS  C:\Users\ldebo\AppData\Local\Temp\ccAQ5mmN.s 			page 4


 160:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	uint32_t lowCount;
 161:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	do {
 162:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		resVal = SYSTEMTIMER->TimerHi; 								// Read Arm system timer high count
 163:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		lowCount = SYSTEMTIMER->TimerLo;							// Read Arm system timer low count
 164:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	} while (resVal != (uint64_t)SYSTEMTIMER->TimerHi);				// Check hi counter hasn't rolled in that t
 165:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	resVal = (uint64_t)resVal << 32 | lowCount;						// Join the 32 bit values to a full 64 bit
 166:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	return(resVal);													// Return the uint64_t timer tick count
 167:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** }
 168:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 
 169:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** /*-[timer_Wait]-------------------------------------------------------------}
 170:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  This will simply wait the requested number of microseconds before return.
 171:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  02Jul17 LdB
 172:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  --------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
 173:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** void timer_wait (uint64_t us) {
 174:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	us += timer_getTickCount();										// Add current tickcount onto delay
 175:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	while (timer_getTickCount() < us) {};							// Loop on timeout function until timeout
 176:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** }
 177:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 
 178:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 
 179:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** /*-[tick_Difference]--------------------------------------------------------}
 180:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  Given two timer tick results it returns the time difference between them.
 181:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  02Jul17 LdB
 182:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  --------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
 183:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** uint64_t tick_difference (uint64_t us1, uint64_t us2) {
 184:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	if (us1 > us2) {												// If timer one is greater than two then timer rolled
 185:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		uint64_t td = UINT64_MAX - us1 + 1;							// Counts left to roll value
 186:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		return us2 + td;											// Add that to new count
 187:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	} 
 188:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	return us2 - us1;												// Return difference between values
 189:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** }

 194:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 
 195:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** #define MAIL_EMPTY	0x40000000		/* Mailbox Status Register: Mailbox Empty */
 196:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** #define MAIL_FULL	0x80000000		/* Mailbox Status Register: Mailbox Full  */
 197:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 
 198:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** /*-[mailbox_write]----------------------------------------------------------}
 199:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  This will execute the sending of the given data block message thru the
 200:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  mailbox system on the given channel.
 201:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  RETURN: True for success, False for failure.
 202:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  04Jul17 LdB
 203:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  --------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
 204:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** bool mailbox_write (MAILBOX_CHANNEL channel, uint32_t message) {
 205:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	uint32_t value;													// Temporary read value
 206:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	if (channel > MB_CHANNEL_GPU)  return false;					// Channel error
 207:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	message &= ~(0xF);												// Make sure 4 low channel bits are clear 
 208:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	message |= channel;												// OR the channel bits to the value							
 209:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	do {
 210:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		value = MAILBOX->Status1;									// Read mailbox1 status from GPU	
 211:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	} while ((value & MAIL_FULL) != 0);								// Make sure arm mailbox is not full
 212:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	MAILBOX->Write1 = message;										// Write value to mailbox
 213:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	return true;													// Write success
 214:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** }
 215:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 
 216:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** /*-[mailbox_read]-----------------------------------------------------------}
AARCH64 GAS  C:\Users\ldebo\AppData\Local\Temp\ccAQ5mmN.s 			page 5


 217:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  This will read any pending data on the mailbox system on the given channel.
 218:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  RETURN: The read value for success, 0xFEEDDEAD for failure.
 219:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  04Jul17 LdB
 220:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  --------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
 221:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** uint32_t mailbox_read (MAILBOX_CHANNEL channel) {
 222:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	uint32_t value;													// Temporary read value
 223:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	if (channel > MB_CHANNEL_GPU)  return 0xFEEDDEAD;				// Channel error
 224:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	do {
 225:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		do {
 226:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			value = MAILBOX->Status0;								// Read mailbox0 status
 227:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		} while ((value & MAIL_EMPTY) != 0);						// Wait for data in mailbox
 228:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		value = MAILBOX->Read0;										// Read the mailbox	
 229:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	} while ((value & 0xF) != channel);								// We have response back
 230:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	value &= ~(0xF);												// Lower 4 low channel bits are not part of message
 231:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	return value;													// Return the value
 232:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** }

 240:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** /*-[INTERNAL: BoardRevisionCheck ]-----------------------------------------}
 241:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  This will read the board revision from the mailbox system and for Model 1
 242:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  A and B set the activity led GPIO to 16 instead of 47 for later boards.
 243:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  04Jul17 LdB
 244:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  --------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
 245:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** static bool ModelCheckHasRun = false;
 246:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** static int ActivityGPIOPort = 47;
 247:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 
 248:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** static void BoardRevisionCheck (void) {
 249:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	uint32_t __attribute__((aligned(16))) message[7];
 250:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	ModelCheckHasRun = true;										// Set we have run the model check
 251:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	message[0] = sizeof(message);									// Set total message size
 252:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	message[1] = 0;													// Zero response message
 253:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	message[2] = MAILBOX_TAG_GET_BOARD_REVISION;					// Get Board revision tag
 254:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	message[3] = 4;													// Response Buffer length is 4 bytes
 255:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	message[4] = 0;													// Provided data length = 0
 256:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	message[5] = 0;													// Response
 257:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	message[6] = 0;													// END no more tags
 258:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	mailbox_write(MB_CHANNEL_TAGS, ARMaddrToGPUaddr(&message[0]));
 259:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	mailbox_read(MB_CHANNEL_TAGS);									// Write message and clear response
 260:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	if ((message[1] == 0x80000000) && (message[4] == 0x80000004)) {
 261:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		if ((message[5] >= 0x0002) && (message[5] <= 0x000F)){		// Models A, B return 0002 to 000F
 262:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			ActivityGPIOPort = 16;									// GPIO port 16 is activity led
 263:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		} else ActivityGPIOPort = 47;								// GPIO port 47 activity as default
 264:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	}
 265:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** }
 266:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 
 267:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** void set_Activity_LED (bool on) {
 268:rpi-BasicHardware.c ****  
 269:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	switch (RPi_CpuId.PartNumber) {
 270:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		case 0xb76: {												// arm1176jzf-s AKA Pi1
 271:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			if (!ModelCheckHasRun) BoardRevisionCheck();			// Just check board isn't early Pi1 on GPIO16
 272:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			gpio_output(ActivityGPIOPort, on);						// GPIO activity (port 16 or 47 depends on model) on/off
 273:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			break;
AARCH64 GAS  C:\Users\ldebo\AppData\Local\Temp\ccAQ5mmN.s 			page 6


 274:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		}
 275:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		case 0xc07: {												// cortex-a7 AKA Pi2
 276:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			gpio_output(47, on);									// GPIO port 47 on/off
 277:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			break;
 278:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		}
 279:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		case 0xd03: {												// cortex-a53 AKA Pi3 
 280:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			uint32_t __attribute__((aligned(16))) message[8];
 281:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			message[0] = sizeof(message);							// Set total message size
 282:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			message[1] = 0;											// Zero response message
 283:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			message[2] = MAILBOX_TAG_SET_GPIO_STATE;				// Set GPIO state
 284:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			message[3] = 8;											// Response is 8 bytes
 285:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			message[4] = 8;											// Send parameters is 8 bytes
 286:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			message[5] = 130;										// Port 130
 287:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			message[6] = (uint32_t)on;								// Set on/off
 288:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			message[7] = 0;											// END no more tags
 289:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			mailbox_write(MB_CHANNEL_TAGS, ARMaddrToGPUaddr(&message[0]));
 290:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			mailbox_read(MB_CHANNEL_TAGS);							// Write message and clear response
 291:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 			break;
 292:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		}
 293:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	}
 294:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** }
 295:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 
 296:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** void DeadLoop(void) {
 297:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	while (1) {
 298:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		set_Activity_LED(true);
 299:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		timer_wait(500000);				// We want a 0.5 sec delay					
 300:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		set_Activity_LED(false);
 301:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 		timer_wait(500000);				// We want a 0.5 sec delay
 302:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** 	}
 303:rpi-BasicHardware.c **** }

   4:printf_64.inc **** static int skip_atoi(const char **s)
   5:printf_64.inc **** {
   6:printf_64.inc **** 	int i = 0;
   7:printf_64.inc ****

   9:printf_64.inc **** 		i = i * 10 + *((*s)++) - '0';
